Key value 37 + Now try a repeating-key XOR cipher. E.g. it should take a string Ã¢Â€Âœhello worldÃ¢Â€Â and, given the key is Ã¢Â€ÂœkeyÃ¢Â€Â, xor the first letter Ã¢Â€ÂœhÃ¢Â€Â with Ã¢Â€ÂœkÃ¢Â€Â, then xor Ã¢Â€ÂœeÃ¢Â€Â with Ã¢Â€ÂœeÃ¢Â€Â, then Ã¢Â€ÂœlÃ¢Â€Â with Ã¢Â€ÂœyÃ¢Â€Â, and then xor next char Ã¢Â€ÂœlÃ¢Â€Â with Ã¢Â€ÂœkÃ¢Â€Â again, then Ã¢Â€ÂœoÃ¢Â€Â with Ã¢Â€ÂœeÃ¢Â€Â and so on. You may use an index of coincidence, Hamming distance, Kasiski examination, statistical tests or whatever method you feel would show the best result.
